// AGENT IMAGE WATERFALL TEST
// REMOVE AFTER COMPLETION


$(window).load(function(){

var agents = {
  1: 'female-1',
  2: 'female-2',
  3: 'male-1',
  4: 'male-2'
}

function getRandomInt(min, max) {
    return Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1)) + min;
}

var random = getRandomInt(1,4);
var agentSrc= agents[random];

if(localStorage){
  localStorage.chatAgent = `/content/dam/web/en_us/shared/pilot/${agentSrc}-large@2x.jpg`
}

var agentCount = $('.agent-image').length;
if(agentCount <= 0){
  $('.live-chat-container').find('a.chat-trigger').prepend('<img class="agent-image"/>');
  
}


  var smallAgent = localStorage.chatAgent.replace('large', 'small');
  $('.agent-image').attr('src', `${smallAgent}`);

});
</script>

     $CQ(function() {
         var campaignParam = 'campaign',
             experienceParam = 'experience',
             campaignName = CQ.shared.HTTP.getParameter(location.href, campaignParam),
             experienceName = CQ.shared.HTTP.getParameter(location.href, experienceParam),
             allTeasers = [{"path":"/content/www/en_us/home/products/marketing-cloud/overview/jcr:content/main-par/columncontainer_590b/column2_par/columncontainer_3667/column2_par/columncontainer_9e5c/default","url":"/content/www/en_us/home/products/marketing-cloud/overview/jcr:content/main-par/columncontainer_590b/column2_par/columncontainer_3667/column2_par/columncontainer_9e5c.default.html","name":"default","title":"Default","campainName":"","thumbnail":"/products/marketing-cloud/overview/_jcr_content/main-par/columncontainer_590b/column2_par/columncontainer_3667/column2_par/columncontainer_9e5c/.thumb.png"}];

         // if campaign and experience in url params
         // get the specified experience and set it as the default in the allTeasers array
         if (campaignName && experienceName){
             function isForcedTeaser(teaser, campaign, experience){
                 var campaignsDirectory = '/content/campaigns';
                 var pathToCampaign = campaignsDirectory + '/' + campaign;
                 var fullPathToExperience = pathToCampaign + '/' + experience + '/';
                 if(teaser.campaignPath == pathToCampaign){
                     if(teaser.path.startsWith(fullPathToExperience) || teaser.thumbnail.startsWith(fullPathToExperience)){
                         return true;
                     }
                 }
                 return false;
             }
             
             for (i = 0; i < allTeasers.length; i++) {
                 if (isForcedTeaser(allTeasers[i], campaignName, experienceName)) {
                     var forcedTeaser = allTeasers[i];
                     forcedTeaser.name = "default";
                     forcedTeaser.segments = undefined;
                     delete forcedTeaser.segments;
                     allTeasers = [forcedTeaser]; 
                 }
             }
         }
	 
             CQ_Analytics.Engine.loadTeaser({ targetID: "_content_www_en_us_home_products_marketing-cloud_overview_jcr_content_main-par_columncontainer_590b_column2_par_columncontainer_3667_column2_par_columncontainer_9e5c", teasers: allTeasers, strategy: "", trackingURL: null});
	 });
    </script>

	<p><a title="CRM" href="https://www.salesforce.com/crm/">CRM</a>: Salesforce CRM fosters better customer relationships, helping you save money and increase profits.</p>

<p><a title="Sales Forecasting" href="https://www.salesforce.com/sales-cloud/quota-forecasting-software.jsp">Sales Forecasting</a>: Sales forecasting and analytics are some of the many powerful features that Salesforce CRM offers.</p>

<p><a href="https://www.salesforce.com/sales-cloud/email-tracking-software.jsp">Sales Tracking Software</a>: Robust sales tracking features help you analyze sales pipelines, perform win-loss analyses, and more.</p>

<p><a href="/products/service-cloud/overview/">Analytics for Customer Service</a>: Use service analytics to diagnose, react, and fix problems faster with Service Cloud Einstein.</p>

<p><a title="Salesforce Reviews" href="https://www.salesforce.com/customers/reviews/">Salesforce Reviews</a>: Read honest reviews from real Salesforce customers.</p>

<p><a title="Digital Advertising" href="https://www.salesforce.com/marketing-cloud/features/social-advertising-solutions/">Digital Advertising</a>: Advertising solutions that help you securely use your customer data to reach your customers across all channels — at scale.</p>

<p><a href="/products/desk/overview/">Automate Support</a>: Increase productivity with the ability to automate support so that agents can focus on the more complex work at hand.</p>

<p><a href="https://www.salesforce.com/marketing-cloud/features/content-marketing-optimization/">Content Marketing Optimization</a>: Content marketing optimization in a single location for all your cross-channel content for a consistent consumer experience.</p>

<p><a href="/products/sales-cloud/features/marketing-automation-software/">Marketing Automation Software</a>: Marketing automation software resources and knowledge to create better-performing marketing campaigns.</p>
